article row mb-3"><div class="headlines |"><h1 class="headline | font-weight-bold col"><span>Trump hails experimental treatment for his virus recovery </span></h1><h5 class="subheadline | font-weight-light col"><span>\xe2\x80\x98I feel great!\xe2\x80\x99</span></h5></div><div class="lead-art | col-12"><div class="video | pb-3 w-100"><div class="position-relative"><div id="fusion-static-enter:4c8c66be-34cf-47d0-9bcf-9526e3e961ed" style="display:none"></div><div class="goldfish-player"><div id="powa-4c8c66be-34cf-47d0-9bcf-9526e3e961ed" class="absolute powa" class="icon | pinterest pointer" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Share on Pinterest</title><path d="M12 2C6.477 2 2 6.477 2 12c0 4.239 2.634 7.86 6.354 9.317-.09-.79-.165-2.008.033-2.873.18-.781 1.169-4.97 1.169-4.97s-.297-.602-.297-1.482c0-1.391.807-2.428 1.811-2.428.856 0 1.267.642 1.267 1.407 0 .856-.543 2.14-.83 3.334-.24.995.501 1.81 1.48 1.81 1.778 0 3.145-1.876 3.145-4.576 0-2.395-1.72-4.066-4.181-4.066-2.848 0-4.519 2.132-4.519 4.338 0 .856.33 1.777.74 2.28.083.098.091.189.067.288-.074.312-.247.995-.28 1.135-.041.181-.148.223-.338.132-1.25-.584-2.033-2.403-2.033-3.876 0-3.153 2.289-6.05 6.61-6.05 3.465 0 6.164 2.47 6.164 5.778 0 3.449-2.173 6.222-5.185 6.222-1.012 0-1.967-.527-2.288-1.152l-.626 linkedin pointer" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><title>Share on LinkedIn</title><path d="M4.329 3H19.67C20.405 3 21 3.595 21 4.329V19.67c0 .734-.595 1.329-1.329 1.329H4.33A1.329 1.329 0 0 1 3 19.67V4.329C3 3.595 3.595 3 4.329 3zM18.35 17.901v-5.316c0-2.626-1.632-3.522-3.142-3.522-1.396 0-2.31.904-2.572 1.433h-.035V9.305H10V17.9h2.706v-4.66c0-1.243.787-1.847 1.59-1.847.76 0 1.349.427 1.349 1.812v4.695h2.706zM7.56 8.107c.86 0 1.56-.656 1.56-1.553C9.12 5.656 8.42 5 7.56 5 6.697 5 6 5.656 6 6.554c0 .897.698 1.553 1.56 1.553zm-1.354 9.788h2.706V9.298H6.207v8.597z" fill-rule="evenodd"></path></svg></div></div></div></section><section class="body | w-100"><div class="article-body | article w-100"><p class="text | article-text">WASHINGTON (AP) \xe2\x80\x94 President Donald Trump on Wednesday credited an experimental drug treatment with helping his recovery from COVID-19 and suggested his diagnosis could be a \xe2\x80\x9cblessing in disguise\xe2\x80\x9d in the nation\xe2\x80\x99s battle against the pandemic. But there is no way for the president or his doctors to know whether the drug had any effect.</p><p class="text | article-text">In a new White House video posted Wednesday evening, Trump said his illness had shed light on an experimental antibody cocktail that he tied to his improved condition. Seemingly sensitive to the fact that his treatment course has been far more comprehensive than the care received by average Americans, he promised to swiftly get the drug approved for broader use \xe2\x80\x94 and distribute it for free \xe2\x80\x94 even though he does not have the power to order that himself.</p><p class="text | article-text">\xe2\x80\x9cI want everybody to be given the same treatment as your president, because I feel great,\xe2\x80\x9d Trump said in a video from the Rose Garden. \xe2\x80\x9cI feel, like, perfect.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><div class="video | pb-3 w-100"><div class="position-relative"><div id="fusion-static-enter:e3b5e66b-78d9-4fd4-b3d7-5deaccfe61c1" style="display:none"></div><div class="goldfish-player"><div id="powa-e3b5e66b-78d9-4fd4-b3d7-5deaccfe61c1" class="absolute powa" data-ad-bar="false" data-ads="true" data-api="prod" data-aspect-ratio="0.5625" data-autoplay="false" data-env="prod" data-debug="false" data-org="gray" data-ping-rate="15" data-preroll-ad-path="63316753/kmvt/web/politics/national/" data-sticky="true" data-uuid="e3b5e66b-78d9-4fd4-b3d7-5deaccfe61c1"></div></div><div id="fusion-static-exit:e3b5e66b-78d9-4fd4-b3d7-5deaccfe61c1" style="display:none"></div></div></div><div></div><p class="text | article-text">Still, questions continue to swirl about the trajectory of Trump\xe2\x80\x99s recovery and when he might be able to return to normal activities, including campaigning, less than four weeks before Election Day. The video marked Trump\xe2\x80\x99s first appearance before a camera \xe2\x80\x94 albeit a White House-operated one \xe2\x80\x94in nearly two days. The White House has released only limited details about his condition and treatment, leading to questions about what lies ahead for Trump.</p><p class="text | article-text">Trump received an experimental antiviral cocktail made by Regeneron through a \xe2\x80\x9ccompassionate use\xe2\x80\x9d exemption, a recognition of the above-and-beyond standard of care he receives as president. The safety and effectiveness of the drug have not yet been proven. And there is no way for the president or his doctors to know that the drug had any effect. Most people recover from COVID-19.</p><p class="text | article-text">It\xe2\x80\x99s not the first time the president has trumpeted an unproven treatment. He spent months painting the anti-malarial drug hydroxychloroquine as a miracle treatment for the virus \xe2\x80\x94 taking a preventative course himself \xe2\x80\x94 even though experts have said it is not effective against COVID-19.</p><p class="text | article-text">Trump hailed the Regeneron cocktail even as drugmaker Eli Lilly moves forward with its own similar treatment.</p><div></div><p class="text | article-text">Eli Lilly formally asked the Food and Drug Administration on Wednesday to allow emergency use of its experimental antibody based on early results suggesting it reduces symptoms. There is no timetable for the FDA to make a decision, though the agency has moved on such applications within weeks.</p><p class="text | article-text">Lilly says it could supply as many as 1 million doses of its therapy in the final quarter of 2020, with 100,000 available in October. Regeneron, which has not yet applied for FDA clearance, said in July it could have anywhere between 70,000 and 1.3 million doses of its therapy available by the fall, depending on dosage and medical use, under a contract from the federal government.</p><p class="text | article-text">The company said this advance production would allow the treatment to be distributed \xe2\x80\x9cimmediately\xe2\x80\x9d if it were authorized by the FDA. A company spokesperson did not immediately respond to a request for comment Wednesday.</p><p class="text | article-text">In the video, Trump continued to play down the threat of the virus, promising those who are ill that they\xe2\x80\x99re going to \xe2\x80\x9cget better fast, just like I did.\xe2\x80\x9d More than 200,000 people in the U.S. and more than a million worldwide have died from the disease.</p><div></div><p class="text | article-text">Trump posted the video on Twitter not long after aides said he had spent time in the Oval Office for briefings on Hurricane Delta, which is bearing down on the U.S. Gulf Coast, and on economic stimulus prospects \xe2\x80\x94- despite still being contagious two days after he was discharged from Walter Reed National Military Medical Center,</p><p class="text | article-text">Aides insisted that only limited staff were around him and that he entered the office from the outside to limit exposure.</p><p class="text | article-text">With national and battleground public opinion polls showing he faces an uphill fight to winning a second term, Trump spent much of his day on Twitter, throwing broadsides against Democrats and <a href="https://apnews.com/article/virus-outbreak-donald-trump-archive-nancy-pelosi-airlines-81083d06d7709e1ead58205e5ed005c5">pushing lawmakers to take up piecemeal economic aid proposals</a> after nixing negotiations on a broader assistance package.</p><p class="text | article-text">Trump\xe2\x80\x99s doctor reported that the president continued to make progress in his recovery.</p><div></div><p class="text | article-text">Dr. Sean Conley, the White House physician, said Trump had begun the day by declaring, \xe2\x80\x9cI feel great!\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p class="text | article-text">Conley added in a memo that Trump had been symptom-free for over 24 hours, and that his oxygen saturation level and respiratory rate were normal. The memo also said a blood test Monday showed Trump had coronavirus antibodies, substances that fight infection, but he had been given an experimental drug on Friday containing these.</p><p class="text | article-text">Regeneron says it\xe2\x80\x99s not possible for this type of blood test to distinguish between antibodies Trump\xe2\x80\x99s body may be making and those supplied by the company\xe2\x80\x99s drug. Most likely, the ones detected in the Monday test are from the drug, the company said.</p><p class="text | article-text">The Centers for Disease Control and Prevention says individuals can discontinue isolation 10 days after symptom onset. While reports of reinfection are rare, the CDC recommends that even people who recover from COVID-19 continue to wear a mask, stay distanced and follow other precautions.</p><div></div><p class="text | article-text">Doctors said Trump began showing mild symptoms on Oct. 1.</p><div data-oembed-type="twitter" class="oembed | article-oembed w-100 oembed-twitter d-flex justify-content-center"><blockquote class="twitter-tweet"><p lang="en" dir="ltr">A Wednesday update from President <a href="https://twitter.com/realDonaldTrump?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">@realDonaldTrump</a>\xe2\x80\x99s physician: <a href="https://t.co/IEn3Clv9yg">pic.twitter.com/IEn3Clv9yg</a></p>&mdash; Kayleigh McEnany (@PressSec) <a href="https://twitter.com/PressSec/status/1313884629791911937?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw">October 7, 2020</a></blockquote>\n<script async src="https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js" charset="utf-8"></script>\n</div><p class="text | article-text">Access to Trump for White House aides has been extremely limited since his discharge. White House chief of staff Mark Meadows and senior adviser Dan Scavino were among those with the president in the Oval Office, according to officials. Those meeting with Trump are required to wear full personal protective gear to minimize their risk.</p><p class="text | article-text">Trump could have received his briefings elsewhere in the complex, but the president believed it was important that he be seen working from the Oval, according to a White House official who was not authorized to comment publicly and spoke on condition of anonymity.</p><p class="text | article-text">The president has also begun pondering a resumption of travel and is considering hitting the road next week before the scheduled Oct. 15 presidential debate in Miami. White House officials are confident that Trump will be healthy enough to take part in the debate, and are exploring the prospect of travel earlier depending on the course of his recovery.</p><div></div><p class="text | article-text">Elsewhere in the government, the virus is threatening the top ranks of the U.S. military.</p><p class="text | article-text">The assistant commandant of the Marine Corps, <a href="https://apnews.com/article/virus-outbreak-archive-gary-l-thomas-coast-guard-59e19109d15d6f10eeb0417ec961d80d">Gen. Gary L. Thomas, tested positive</a> for the coronavirus, days after he and members of the Joint Chiefs of Staff were in a Pentagon meeting with a Coast Guard leader who was infected with the virus, the service confirmed Wednesday.</p><p class="text | article-text">Thomas attended a meeting of the Joint Chiefs on Friday. The nation\xe2\x80\x99s top military leaders \xe2\x80\x94 including the chairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff, Gen. Mark Milley, and the vice chairman, Gen. John Hyten \xe2\x80\x94 are in quarantine after exposure at that meeting to Adm. Charles W. Ray, the vice commandant of the Coast Guard, who has since tested positive.</p><p class="text | article-text">Amid the national public health crisis, a personal one, and warning flares from leading economists that the virus-scarred economy badly needs stimulus, Trump pushed out about 60 tweets by early evening praising supporters and eviscerating his opponents.</p><div></div><p class="text | article-text">While Trump continues to minimize the threat of the virus, more aides have been testing positive \xe2\x80\x94 including one of his closest advisers, Stephen Miller, who was diagnosed Tuesday. All told, more than a dozen White House staffers have tested positive.</p><p class="text | article-text">Nonetheless, Trump pushed out video of South Dakota Gov. Kristi Noem speaking of her decision to resist COVID-19 restrictions in her state. He also thanked a supporter who tweeted she \xe2\x80\x9cwould wade though a sea of COVID infested water to vote for President Trump on November 3rd.\xe2\x80\x9d</p><p class="text | article-text">___</p><p class="text | article-text">Associated Press writers Marilynn Marchione in Milwaukee and Lauran Neergaard, Zeke Miller, Lolita C. Baldor and Jonathan Lemire in Washington contributed to this report.</p><p class="text | article-text"><i>Copyright 2020 The Associated Press. All rights reserved.</i></p></div></section><section class="recommendations | w-100"><div id="fusion-static-enter:68002c00-f535-4894-9a46-232aa26343d5" style="display:none"></div><div class="connatix
